The windows of the restaurant have also become picture frames. When you look over, there is a vertical version of a picture of green mountains and green bamboos. Outside the window of the bar is no exception, there is a picture of listening to frogs in a lotus pond.

If we must come to Guilin once, then this time we will come to the destination of Guilin. During the day, we went to see mountains and rivers, and then came back to Jiurang. Haha, we were still in the mountains and rivers. I don‚Äôt dare to stay in Guilin for a long time. After a long time, I will be reluctant to leave. msg:Let me write a review from the bottom of my heart. One is Guangzhou Jumeirah. At that time, I said that the hotel‚Äôs breakfast was prepared so well. The management of the hotel was absolutely attentive. A hotel that pursues the ultimate in dishes and utensils. It took three months to prepare an afternoon handmade tea stand. The same style in Aman, Tokyo. It is the first time I have seen such a heart in so many luxury hotels in China. From the housekeeper to pick up the luggage, the natural and clean feeling, the fruit and nut ritual on the car is really attentive, and the luggage is directly connected to the room when the hotel arrives. This connection is really praised and enters the lobby fragrance music , An instant immersion, the housekeeper introduced that it is specially made by the same manufacturer of Aman in Shanghai. Each work has a name, with the ultimate intent. Each one is carefully selected, and I have the urge to taste it. There is always one I like, by the way Now, I like a coconut water in the refrigerator. The butler is very considerate. After check-in, they will be delivered directly to the guest room. They asked about the turn-down time and snack delivery time. The breakfast quality is very good. You can eat everything from local rice noodles to steamed buns, pancakes and fruits. In the afternoon, I also ate the free New Chilan ice cream provided by the hotel. There was no limit! For dinner, I ordered the smoked and vinegar blood duck recommended by the chef. It was mixed with the smell of smoke, which was much better than what I had eaten in Guilin! It can be seen that the hotel is very attentive in many aspects, ingenuity and quality, the design is very good and quiet, and the lighting and music at night are very good.
